style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构消费者权益保护工作开展情况和整体状况作</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >出</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >综合评价</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >的监管过程</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第三条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保监管评价对象为在中华人民共和国境内依法设立的向消费者提供金融产品或服务的银行保险机构。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第四条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保监管评价</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >是银行业保险业</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >行为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >监管的重要组成部分，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >应充分体现</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >行为监管</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >的特点和要求，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >兼顾机构体制机制</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >建设</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >和具体</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >操作执行</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >将</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >定性和定量评价有机结合</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，遵循依法依规、客观公正、科学规范、突出重点的原则。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:31.4500pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=center  style="text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:center;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >第二章</font>  <font face="宋体" >评价要素和等级</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:31.4500pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第五条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保监管评价</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >要素</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >包括</font>&#8220;体制建设&#8221;&#8220;机制与运行&#8221;&#8220;操作与服务&#8221;&#8220;教育宣传&#8221;&#8220;纠纷化解&#8221;5项基本要素和&#8220;监督检查&#8221;1项调减要素。5项基本要素总权重为100%。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）体制建设。主要评价</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消费者权益保护工作相关</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >公司治理和组织架构建设等情况。该要素权重为</font>10%。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）机制与运行。主要评价银行保险机构消费者权益保护工作机制建设和运行情况，包括消费者权益保护审查、信息披露、个人信息保护、内部培训、内部考核、内部审计等。该要素权重为</font>25%。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）操作与服务。主要评价银行保险机构日常经营和服务中对消费者权益保护有关要求的落实情况，包括但不限于营销宣传、适当性管理、销售行为管控、合作机构管理、服务质量与收费等。该要素权重为</font>30%。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（四）教育宣传。主要评价银行保险机构消费者教育宣传总体安排、集中教育宣传活动、常态化消费者教育工作开展情况等。该要素权重为</font>10%。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1;" ><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><span style='mso-list:Ignore;' >（五）</span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >纠纷化解。主要评价银行保险机构投诉管理、投诉数量以及纠纷多元化解机制落实情况。该要素权重为</font>25%。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（六）监督检查。根据银行保险机构消费者权益保护现场检查、举报调查、投诉督查、复议诉讼情况以及日常舆情、重大负面事件和机构相关整改落实情况进行调减，幅度不超过总权重的</font>25%。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第六条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保监管评价各要素下设若干评价指标。银保监会根据行为监管特点，立足行业发展和消费者权益保护工作实际，对消保监管评价要素下设的具体评价指标进行动态调整</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第七条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保监管评价计分包括：指标得分、要素得分和总体得分。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）指标得分。针对每一评价要素中的不同评价指标评分。在指标得分区间内，根据工作开展情况确定得分。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）要素得分。每一评价要素得分为该要素下不同评价指标得分之和。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）总体得分。评价总体得分为</font>5项基本要素得分和1项调减要素得分加总之和。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第八条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保监管评价总分值为</font>100分，最小计分单位为0.1分。根据最终总体得分，消保监管评价结果分为四个等级。等级数字越大表示机构消费者权益保护工作存在的问题越多，需要越高程度的监管关注。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保监管评价总体得分在</font>90分（含）以上为一级；75分（含）至90分为二级,其中：85分（含）至90分为二级A，80分（含）至85分为二级B，75分（含）至80分为二级C；60分（含）至75分为三级，其中：70分（含）至75分为三级A，65分（含）至70分为三级B，60分（含）至65分为三级C；60分以下为四级。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:31.4500pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=center  style="text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:center;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >第三章</font>  <font face="宋体" >职责分工和操作流程</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=center  style="margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:0.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:center;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第九条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保监管评价周期为一年，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >评价期间为评价年度</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >月</font>1日至当年</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >12</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >月</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >31</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >日。年度监管评价工作原则上应于评价期间结束后</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >个月内完成。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第十条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会负责组织、督导全国银行业保险业消保监管评价工作，并对直接监管的银行保险法人机构开展评价。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第十一条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会派出机构按照属地监管原则，负责对辖内银行保险法人机构和一级分支机构开展消保监管评价，并将一级分支机构的评价结果和同类机构排名报送相关法人监管机构消费者权益保护职能部门。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第十二条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保监管评价流程包括：方案制定、机构自评、评价实施、档案归集。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第十三条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会每年根据消费者权益保护监管工作重点、银行保险机构消费者权益保护工作开展情况等因素，制定年度消保监管评价方案，明确当年消保监管评价具体指标、评分细则和具体时间安排等内容。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >年度消保监管评价方案原则上于评价年度结束前发布。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第十四条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >机构自评。根据银保监会年度消保监管评价方案，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构就</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >项基本要素开展自评，全面客观评价本机构消费者权益保护工作整体效果，将自评结果和每项评价指标自评所依据的证明材料报送相关监管机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第十五条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >评价实施。银保监会及其派出机构开展消保监管评价，应全面收集信息，客观分析评价，参考自评情况，形成评价结果。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）收集信息。银保监会及其派出机构开展消保监管评价应收集的信息包括：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >日常监管过程中掌握的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >与消费者权益保护工作相关的非现场监管和现场检查信息，消费者投诉及处理情况，消费者权益保护相关举报、复议、诉讼、案件以及日常舆情、重大负面事件等信息，银行保险机构报送的自评情况及相关证明材料，行业组织等相关机构关于行业服务质量的评测情况，消保监管评价相关的其他信息。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）综合分析。银保监会及其派出机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >应结合所掌握的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消费者权益保护工作相关的各类信息，进行全面、客观分析，对每项评价要素和指标做出综合评估，形成评价结果。必要时，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >可以通过现场调查、抽查、监管会谈等方式</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >进行核查</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）确定结果。银保监会及其派出机构应综合银行保险机构法人及各一级分支机构的评价结果，将一级分支机构平均得分和法人评价得分按</font>40%和60%进行加权平均</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，得出银行保险机构的总体得分</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >自评得分严重偏离</font>5项基本要素监管评价得分的，将视当年同类机构平均偏离情况扣减总体得分。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（四）结果通报。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会及其派出机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >应适时总结辖内银行业保险业消保监管评价总体情况，在行业内通报，并可通过会谈、监管会议、监管通报等形式向被评机构通报</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >评价结果。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >机构不得</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >广告、宣传、营销等商业目的将评</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >价</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >结果</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >对外披露。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第十六条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >档案归集。消保监管评价结束后，银保监会及其派出机构应对评价过程中生成的重要信息做好归档工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:31.4500pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=center  style="text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:center;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >第四章</font>  <font face="宋体" >评价结果及运用</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:0.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第十七条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会及其派出机构应当充分利用消保监管评价结果</font>,将其作为制定消费者权益保护监管政策与工作规划的重要依据，以及配置监管资源和采取监管措施的重要参考，</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >深入分析</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构消费者权益保护工作存在的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >问题及其成因，督促</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >对发现的问题及时整改。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第十八条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >评价结果。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）评价结果为一级，表明机构消费者权益保护工作在行业内处于领先水平，对消费者权益保护工作的重要性有充分认识，消费者权益保护工作组织架构健全，各项工作机制运行顺畅，能够保障在经营管理和业务环节中落实消费者保护理念和要求。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）评价结果为二级，表明机构消费者权益保护工作在行业内处于中等水平，消费者权益保护工作组织架构比较合理，各项工作机制基本能够保障在大部分经营管理和业务环节中落实消费者保护理念和要求，但工作存在一定不足，需予以改进。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）评价结果为三级，表明机构消费者权益保护工作在行业内处于偏下水平，消费者权益保护工作组织架构建设和各项工作机制运行存在较大问题，经营管理和业务环节中消费者权益保护理念和要求落实不到位，需要及时采取措施提高体制机制执行力，弥补工作缺陷。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（四）评价结果为四级，表明机构消费者权益保护工作在行业内处于落后水平，消费者权益保护工作组织架构建设和各项工作机制运行存在严重问题，难以保障在经营管理和业务环节中落实消费者权益保护要求，侵害消费者合法权益事件屡次发生，必须立即全面检视问题，采取有效措施进行整改。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第十九条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >评价结果</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >通报</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >后，银行保险机构应当针对自身消费者权益保护工作存在的问题和缺陷</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，研究</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >整改措施、</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >提出</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >整改方案</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >评价结果为三级和四级的机构，应</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >于</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >收到评价结果后尽快形成整改计划，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >并于</font>90日内</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >向相关监管机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >提交整改情况</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >进展</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >报告。对于短期内难以完成的整改工作，银行保险机构应当制定</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >阶段性整改台账</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，有序推进。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会及其派出机构应当根据消保监管评价结果，依法对银行保险机构采取差异化监管措施。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）对评价结果为一级的机构，应指导督促其加强日常经营行为管理，有效防范操作风险。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）对评价结果为二级的机构，应关注其消费者权益保护工作薄弱环节，通过窗口指导、监管谈话等方式督促其加强日常经营行为管理，有效防范操作风险。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）对评价结果为三级的机构，除可采取对二级机构的监管措施外，还可视情形</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >依法采取下发风险提示函</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >、</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >监管通报</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >、</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >责令限期整改、责令内部问责</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >等方式要求其强化消费者权益保护体制机制建设和执行，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >必要时公开披露其不当行为。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（四）对评价结果为四级的机构，除可采取对三级机构的监管措施外，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >对</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >于整改措施不力或到期仍无明显整改效果的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >可</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >根据</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >有关法律法规</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >依法在开办新业务、增设分支机构等方面采取相关监管措施。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >对于评价</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >结果为三级及以下或在同类机构中排名持续下降的机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，银保监会及其派出机构应增加现场检查频率，并要求机构进一步提高消费者权益保护内部考核在其综合绩效考评体系中的权重。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:31.4500pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=center  style="text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:center;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >第五章</font>  <font face="宋体" >组织保障和工作要求</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:31.4500pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十一条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会及其派出机构消费者权益保护职能部门负责牵头开展消保监管评价工作，包括：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）组织实施消保监管评价具体工作；</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）对下辖派出机构的消保监管评价工作进行指导和监督；</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >整理消保监管评价档案，做好归档工作</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >；</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（四）根据评价结果对银行保险机构采取后续监管措施</font>;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（五）其他有关消保监管评价的工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十二条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会及其派出机构其他相关部门就消保监管评价工作提供有关信息、资料和建议，并</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >配合消费者权益保护职能部门</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >,根据评价结果对银行保险机构采取后续监管措施。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十三条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会派出机构可根据工作需要，成立消保监管评价工作委员会，对本级派出机构的评价工作进行指导和监督</font>,</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >并通过会议或传签的形式确定评价结果。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十四条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >应当真实、准确、完整地提供</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >监管</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >评价</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >所需数据以及</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >相关材料</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >提交虚假材料</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >的，银保监会及其派出机构应</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >根据具体情节和性质，按照《中华人民共和国银行业监督管理法》</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >《中华人民共和国保险法》</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >相关条款进行严肃处理。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十五条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >消保监管评价应积极利用信息化手段，搭建监管评价信息系统，依托系统集中统一开展数据收集、指标统计、数据分析、结果运用等工作，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >增强规范性和准确性</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十六条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会派出机构应及时将辖内银行保险机构的消保监管评价结果逐级报送上级监管机构消费者权益保护职能部门。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十七条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会及其派出机构应当严格控制评价信息和资料知悉范围，做好消保监管评价信息和资料保密工作。参与消保监管评价的工作人员不得泄露评价过程中获悉的国家秘密、商业秘密、敏感信息和个人信息。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十八条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >评价工作结束后，发现银行保险机构在评价期间内存在重大违法违规问题，严重侵害消费者合法权益的，银保监会及其派出机构可视情形对评价结果进行调级调档，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >并将调整情况逐级报送上级监管机构消费者权益保护职能部门</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:31.4500pt;mso-char-indent-count:0.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=center  style="text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:center;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >第六章</font>  <font face="宋体" >附则</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:31.4500pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十九条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >本办法规定的消保监管评价对象不包含开发银行、政策性银行、</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >金融资产管理公司、金融资产投资公司、</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >金融租赁公司、</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >企业集团财务公司、</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >货币经纪公司、省联社、贷款公司、农村资金互助社、政策性保险公司、保险集团</font>(控股)公司、再保险公司、农业保险公司、养老保险公司、相互保险组织、保险资产管理公司、养老金管理公司和保险专业中介机构。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第三十条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >不开展个人业务或者个人业务占比较小的外资法人银行、外国银行分行等可不作为消保监管评价对象。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第三十一条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >截至评价年度末，开业不满</font>2个会计年度的银行保险机构不作为消保监管评价对象。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第三十二条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >对于农村中小银行，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会派出机构每年</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >可根据工作实际，仅对法人机构开展评价，并自行确定机构覆盖范围。原则上应</font>5年全覆盖，每年覆盖率不低于20%。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第三十三条</font></span><span ></w:LsdException></w:LatentStyles></xml><![endif]--><style>@font-face{font-family:"Times New Roman";}@font-face{font-family:"宋体";}@font-face{font-family:"Wingdings";}@font-face{font-family:"仿宋_GB2312";}p.MsoNormal{mso-style-name:正文;mso-style-parent:"";margin:0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:'Times 5.4000pt 0.0000pt 5.4000pt;mso-para-margin:0pt;mso-para-margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-ansi-language:#0400;mso-fareast-language:#0400;mso-bidi-language:#0400;}@page{mso-page-border-surround-header:no;	mso-page-border-surround-footer:no;}@page Section0{margin-top:72.0000pt;margin-bottom:72.0000pt;margin-left:90.0000pt;margin-right:90.0000pt;size:595.3000pt 841.9000pt;layout-grid:15.6000pt;}div.Section0{page:Section0;}</style></head><body style="tab-interval:21pt;text-justify-trim:punctuation;" ><!--StartFragment--><div class="Section0"  style="layout-grid:15.6000pt;" ><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >各银保监局（辽宁、广西、海南、宁夏除外）：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >近年来，部分信托公司通过非金融子公司进行监管套利、隐匿风险；开展违规关联交易、进行不当利益输送，给信托业发展造成潜在风险。为治理市场乱象，助力打好防范化解金融风险攻坚战，促进信托业改革和转型发展，现就清理规范信托公司非金融子公司业务的有关事项通知如下：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >一、本通知所指信托公司境内一级非金融子公司，是指信托公司在境内以固有资产直接投资设立或以投资资管产品等方式间接投资设立的，具有控制权且未持有金融业务许可证的公司。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >二、自本通知印发之日起，信托公司不得新增境内一级非金融子公司，已设立的境内一级非金融子公司不得新增对境内外企业的投资。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >三、信托公司可选择保留一家目前经营范围涵盖投资管理或资产管理类业务的境内一级非金融子公司。该公司仅可作为私募基金管理人受托管理私募股权投资基金，且不得控制、共同控制被投资方或对被投资方施加重大影响，不得参与被投资方的日常经营，投资年限不得超过</font>5年。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >前款中</font>&#8220;控制、共同控制被投资方或对被投资方施加重大影响&#8221;，根据《企业会计准则》有关规定进行判断。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >基金业务不符合本条要求的，到期后不得直接或变相新增和续作，其余业务在合同期满或项目结束后不得继续开展。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >四、信托公司应当有计划地以转让股权等方式清理对以下企业的投资，清理期限不得超过</font>3年：一是信托公司按照本通知第三条规定选择保留的境内一级非金融子公司在境内外投资的企业；二是信托公司其余境内一级非金融子公司及其在境内外投资的企业。上述企业有存续基金业务的，应当于相关项目清算后1年内完成清理。清理工作完成前，上述企业原则上不得新增业务。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >清理确有困难的，信托公司应当在清理期限届满前</font>2个月向属地银保监局提交延长清理期限报告。清理延期不得超过一次，延长期限不得超过1年。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >五、信托公司应当全面梳理境内一级非金融子公司及其在境内外投资企业的基本情况，合理拟定清理规范工作方案，列明时间节点安排，明确存续子公司并表管理措施等，并于</font>4个月内将方案报送至属地银保监局，经审查后实施。各信托公司应当加强存续非金融子公司并表管理，按季度向属地银保监局报送方案实施进展情况，并在依法合规完成清理规范工作后，及时上报经董事长签字确认的工作报告。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >六、各银保监局应当切实承担属地监管责任，加强全程督导跟踪，认真审查方案内容，严防信息漏报瞒报；通过现场检查、督导等方式，适时查验阶段性工作进展与质量；加强辖内信托公司并表监管，发现非金融子公司与母公司之间违法违规交易行为的，依法依规对信托公司采取监管措施或进行行政处罚；清理规范工作完成后，组织专项验收，并向银保监会报送正式报告。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >七、本通知中</font>&#8220;企业&#8221;的组织形式适用《中华人民共和国公司法》《中华人民共和国合伙企业法》等法律的规定。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=justify  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-left:0.0000gd;text-indent:30.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:30.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  align=right
