style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;mso-hansi-font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2021</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;mso-hansi-font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >年</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;mso-hansi-font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >7</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;mso-hansi-font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >月</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;mso-hansi-font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >30</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;mso-hansi-font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >日</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;mso-hansi-font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br clear=all style='page-break-before:always'></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;mso-hansi-font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=16  align=right  style="text-align:right;line-height:31.0000pt;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;mso-hansi-font-family:仿宋;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=16  align=center  style="text-align:center;line-height:32.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:方正小标宋_GBK;font-size:22.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="方正小标宋_GBK" >中国银行保险监督管理委员会</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:方正小标宋_GBK;font-size:22.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=16  align=center  style="text-align:center;line-height:32.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:方正小标宋_GBK;font-size:22.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="方正小标宋_GBK" >派出机构监管职责规定</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:方正小标宋_GBK;font-size:22.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=16  style="line-height:32.0000pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第一条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >为明确中国银行保险监督管理委员会（以下简称银保监会）派出机构监管职责，根据《中华人民共和国银行业监督管理法》《中华人民共和国商业银行法》《中华人民共和国保险法》等法律、行政法规，制定本规定。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >本规定所称派出机构，是指银保监会派驻各省（自治区、直辖市）和计划单列市的监管局（</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >以下</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >简称银保监局）、派驻地市（州、盟）的监管分局（</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >以下</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >简称银保监分局）以及设在县（市、区、旗）的监管组。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >本规定所称</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >是指依法由银行保险监督管理机构监管的商业银行、政策性银行、开发性银行、农村合作银行、村镇银行、外国银行分行、外国银行代表处、农村信用社、农村资金互助社、贷款公司、保险集团（控股）公司、保险公司、外国保险机构驻华代表机构、保险资产管理公司、保险代理机构、保险经纪机构、保险公估机构、信托公司、金融资产管理公司、金融资产投资公司、金融租赁公司、企业集团财务公司、消费金融公司、汽车金融公司、</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行理财公司</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >、货币经纪公司等机构。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第三条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会对派出机构实行垂直领导。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >派出机构监管职责的确立，遵循职权法定、属地监管、分级负责、权责统一的原则。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局在银保监会的领导下，履行所在省（自治区、直辖市）和计划单列市银行业和保险业监督管理职能。银保监局根据银保监会的授权和统一领导，依法依规独立对辖内银行业</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >和</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >保险业实行统一监督管理。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监分局在银保监局的领导下，履行所在地市银行业和保险业监督管理职能。银保监分局根据银保监会和省（自治区、直辖市）银保监局的授权和统一领导，依法依规独立对辖内银行业和保险业实行统一监督管理。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >县（市、区、旗）监管组在银保监局或银保监分局的授权和统一领导下，依法依规负责所在县市</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >及其业务活动的监管工作，收集所在县市有关金融风险的信息并向上级机构报告，承担交办的其他工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第四条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >派出机构在履行职责过程中坚持和加强党对银行业和保险业监管工作的集中统一领导，确保党中央关于银行业和保险业监管工作的方针政策和决策部署得到贯彻落实。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第五条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >派出机构依法、公开、公正履行对辖内银行业和保险业的监管职责，维护银行业和保险业金融活动当事人的合法权益，促进辖内银行业和保险业合法、稳健运行，防范和化解金融风险等。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第六条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >派出机构根据有关规定统计辖内</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >有关数据和信息，跟踪、监测、研判辖内银行业和保险业运行情况，报送辖内银行业和保险业运行情况和风险情况，及时向上级监管机构报告有可能影响当地银行业和保险业稳健运行的重大事项。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第七条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监会依照法律法规统一监督管理全国银行业和保险业。银保监会可以根据实际需要，明确银保监会直接监管的机构，并在官方网站公布各</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >法人的监管责任单位。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局根据法律、行政法规及银保监会的规定，负责辖内</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >的直接监管，具体名单由银保监局、银保监分局公布。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第八条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:楷体_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" > </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" > <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局依照法定权限和程序制定涉及辖内银行业和保险业监管的规范性文件，并负责监督相关法律、行政法规及规章制度在辖内的贯彻实施。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第九条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局根据法律、行政法规和银保监会的规定，依法对辖内</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >及其有关人员实施行政许可。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >的公司治理、风险管理、内部控制、资本充足、偿付能力、资产质量、业务活动、信息披露、信息科技、第三方合作等实施监督管理，具体监管事项依照法律、行政法规和银保监会的相关规定确定。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >有关风险。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal >银保监局、银保监分局根据法律、行政法规和银保监会的规定，负责辖内信访、银行保险违法行为举报处理以及消费投诉督查等工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >上级监管机构发现下级监管机构负责监管的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >出现下列情形时，应当督促下级监管机构加强监管，情节严重的，可以上收监管权限：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）风险状况急剧恶化；</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）存在重大违法违规问题；</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）上级监管机构认为需要上收监管权限的其他情况。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十三条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >上级监管机构可以依法委托下级监管机构实施监管行为，并负责监督委托实施的行为，对委托实施行为的后果承担法律责任。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >设有银保监分局的银保监局负责审理以辖内银保监分局为被申请人的行政复议案件。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十五条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局负责涉及本机构的各类诉讼的应诉工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十六条</font> </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" > <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局在监管职责范围内与辖区司法机关建立协助机制，依法处理司法机关来访、来函等事项。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局负责建立和完善与辖区公安机关、纪检监察机关</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >协作配合机制，按照规定向公安机关、纪检监察机关通报和移送</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >违法犯罪案件线索，配合公安机关、纪检监察机关开展调查工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十七条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局按照银保监会的统一部署，支持辖内相关自律组织等发挥金融纠纷调解作用，监督辖区银行业</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >和</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >保险业调解机构规范运行，加强与辖区司法机关、司法行政机关、仲裁机构的联系，推动建立完善多元化金融纠纷解决机制。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十八条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局依法依规协同配合做好辖内银行业</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >和</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >保险业风险防范和化解工作，切实承担监管责任，推动落实地方党委党的领导责任、地方国有金融资本股东责任和属地金融风险处置责任。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第二十九条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局指导和监督地方金融监管部门相关业务工作，并有权纠正不符合相关监管规则的行为。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第三十条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局负责与辖区地方人民政府相关部门、其他金融管理机构协同推动当地普惠金融发展，指导辖内</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银行保险机构</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >推进小微企业、</font>&#8220;三农&#8221;等普惠金融重点领域工作。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >第三十一条</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >  <font face="仿宋_GB2312" >银保监局、银保监分局依照法律、行政法规和银保监会的规定对辖内银行业保险业社团组织进行指导和监督。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >为贯彻落实《国务院关于深化</font>&#8220;证照分离&#8221;改革进一步激发市场主体发展活力的通知》（国发〔2021〕7号）要求，进一步激发市场主体活力，结合我会监管工作实际，制定本实施方案。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >一、总体要求</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >以习近平新时代中国特色社会主义思想为指导，全面贯彻党的十九大和十九届二中、三中、四中、五中全会精神，认真落实党中央、国务院重大决策部署，持续深化</font>&#8220;放管服&#8221;改革，推进银行业保险业简化审批，优化准入服务，创新和强化事中事后监管，进一步优化营商环境，激发市场主体活力，推动经济高质量发展。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >二、改革范围和内容</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >自</font>2021年7月1日起，在全国范围内，实施涉企经营许可事项全覆盖清单管理，对银行业保险业涉企经营事项采取&#8220;优化审批服务&#8221;的改革方式，推动行政许可减材料、简程序、减环节。在自由贸易试验区内，进一步加大改革试点力度，采取&#8220;审批改为备案&#8221;的改革方式，结合监管实际，将部分银行保险机构分支机构设立、高级管理人员任职资格核准等事项由事前审批改为事后报告，自由贸易试验区所在县、不设区的市、市辖区的其他区域参照执行。分类推进审批制度改革的同时，创新和加强事中事后监管，切实履行监管职责，防止出现监管真空。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >三、在全国范围优化审批服务</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）下放审批事权。一是将政策性保险公司分支机构开业审批权限，由银保监会下放至所在地银保监局。二是将非银保监会直接监管的外资法人银行董事长、行长任职资格核准事权，由银保监会下放至拟任职机构所在地银保监局。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）精简审批材料。一是加强与信用体系建设、政务信息资源共享、电子证照应用推广等改革举措的有效衔接，行政许可中不再要求申请人提供营业执照复印件。二是银行业任职资格核准事项中不再要求拟任人提供个人及其家庭主要成员的征信报告，改为拟任人书面承诺符合相关条件要求。三是提升系统内部数据收集和查询能力，不再要求申请人提供我会向银行保险机构颁发的许可证复印件。四是将</font>&#8220;综合鉴定&#8221;栏目统一纳入任职资格申请表，保险业任职资格核准事项中不再要求申请人提供单独的综合鉴定材料。五是结合审批工作实际，进一步精简部分许可事项申请材料，详见《中央层面设定的涉企经营许可事项改革清单（2021年全国版）》（国发〔2021〕7号文附件1）第398、403、405、417、418项等。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）压减审批环节。一是保险集团（控股）公司、保险公司（含专属自保组织和相互保险组织）因变更名称、股权、注册资本、业务范围等前置审批事项修改公司章程的，章程不需再次报请审批，改为事后报告。二是落实《中国银保监会办公厅关于深化银行业保险业</font>&#8220;放管服&#8221;改革 优化营商环境的通知》（银保监办发〔2020〕129号）要求，取消银行业保险业董事、监事（保险业）和高级管理人员任职资格考试。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（四）压减审批时限。将融资担保公司设立、变更审批事项的审批时限由</font>30日压减至20日。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（五）延长许可证件有效期限。将典当经营许可证的有效期限由</font>6年延长至10年。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-weight:normal;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >四、简化自由贸易试验区准入</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）将自由贸易试验区内中外资银行分行级以下分支机构（不含分行）设立、变更、终止和高级管理人员任职资格核准事项，由事前审批改为事后报告。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）将自由贸易试验区内保险支公司及以下分支机构设立、迁址、撤销和高级管理人员任职资格核准事项，由事前审批改为事后报告。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）贯彻落实简政放权工作精神和</font>&#8220;证照分离&#8221;改革精神，及时总结自由贸易试验区可复制改革试点经验，依法通过修改许可规章制度向全国复制推广。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >五、创新和加强事中事后监管</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）切实做好</font>&#8220;放管结合&#8221;。银保监会及其派出机构、地方金融监督管理部门要按照&#8220;谁审批、谁监管，谁主管、谁监管&#8221;原则，切实履行监管职责，防止出现监管真空。对于下放审批权限的，要同步调整优化监管层级，实现审批监管权责统一。对于事前审批改为事后报告的，要及时明确报告程序和材料目录，督促银行保险机构按规定履行报告手续。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）压实机构主体责任。要求银行保险机构确保相关许可申请材料和报告材料的真实性、完整性、准确性，以及报告所涉机构、高级管理人员的合规性、适格性。对存在未按规定履行报告手续、提交虚假材料等不合规、不审慎行为的机构，依法依规采取监管强制措施、实施行政处罚，同时追究相关责任人责任。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）强化日常监管。创新随机抽查方式方法，结合问题导向和风险导向确定随机抽查项目，在现场检查中扎实推进</font>&#8220;双随机、一公开&#8221;监管。强化科技赋能，依托国家&#8220;互联网+监管&#8221;系统和银保监会非现场监管信息系统，充分利用大数据等技术手段，加强非现场风险监测。对日常监管中发现的违法违规行为，依法严格实施行政处罚。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（四）提升信用监管效能。建立与有关部门的监管协调机制和信息共享机制，依法依规实施守信联合激励和失信联合惩戒。加强银行保险机构董事、监事和高级管理人员信用监管，根据违法违规情形和失信程度，依法对有关人员采取行业通报、社会公示、市场禁入等方式进行处理，强化市场约束和社会监督，督促有关人员依法履职。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:none;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="黑体" >六、组织实施</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:黑体;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（一）加强组织领导。要充分认识</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >深化</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >&#8220;证照分离&#8221;改革工作的重要意义，加强</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >对</font>&#8220;证照分离&#8221;改革工作的组织领导，建立有效的工作机制，做好内部条线的工作对接和业务指导，完善事中事后监管措施，确保各项改革措施落地</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >见效</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。按照改革工作</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >部署</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，</font>&#8220;全国一盘棋&#8221;，</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >控制试点范围</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，确保有计划、高质量完成改革工作</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >，稳妥推进自由贸易试验区审批制度改革</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-right:0.0000pt;mso-para-margin-top:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-right:0.0000gd;mso-para-margin-bottom:0.0000gd;text-indent:36.0000pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0000;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;vertical-align:baseline;line-height:200%;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（二）强化统筹协同。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >统筹</font>&#8220;证照分离&#8221;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >改革</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >与简政放权等工作，放管结合</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >、并重</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >推进</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" >&#8220;互联网+政务服务&#8221;&#8220;互联网+监管&#8221;等系统建设，</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >配合市场监管</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >部门</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >深化商事登记制度改革，配合推进电子证照归集运用，强化</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >上下衔接、内外联动，形成工作合力，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >助力</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >各项改革措施落地。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >（三）</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋_GB2312;line-height:200%;font-size:18.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" ><font face="仿宋_GB2312" >。</font></span><span >重点加强对行政许可受理窗口服务人员和行政许可审批工作人员培训，确保其掌握</font>&#8220;证照分离&#8221;改革工作的实施要求及工作流程，</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　为了防范和处置非法集资，保护社会公众合法权益，防范化解金融风险，维护经济秩序和社会稳定，制定本条例。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第二条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　本条例所称非法集资，是指未经国务院金融管理部门依法许可或者违反国家金融管理规定，以许诺还本付息或者给予其他投资回报等方式，向不特定对象吸收资金的行为。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >非法集资的防范以及行政机关对非法集资的处置，适用本条例。法律、行政法规对非法从事银行、证券、保险、外汇等金融业务活动另有规定的，适用其规定。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >本条例所称国务院金融管理部门，是指中国人民银行、国务院金融监督管理机构和国务院外汇管理部门。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第三条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　本条例所称非法集资人，是指发起、主导或者组织实施非法集资的单位和个人；所称非法集资协助人，是指明知是非法集资而为其提供帮助并获取经济利益的单位和个人。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第四条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　国家禁止任何形式的非法集资，对非法集资坚持防范为主、打早打小、综合治理、稳妥处置的原则。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第五条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　省、自治区、直辖市人民政府对本行政区域内防范和处置非法集资工作负总责，地方各级人民政府应当建立健全政府统一领导的防范和处置非法集资工作机制。县级以上地方人民政府应当明确防范和处置非法集资工作机制的牵头部门（以下简称处置非法集资牵头部门），有关部门以及国务院金融管理部门分支机构、派出机构等单位参加工作机制；乡镇人民政府应当明确牵头负责防范和处置非法集资工作的人员。上级地方人民政府应当督促、指导下级地方人民政府做好本行政区域防范和处置非法集资工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >行业主管部门、监管部门应当按照职责分工，负责本行业、领域非法集资的防范和配合处置工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第六条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　国务院建立处置非法集资部际联席会议（以下简称联席会议）制度。联席会议由国务院银行保险监督管理机构牵头，有关部门参加，负责督促、指导有关部门和地方开展防范和处置非法集资工作，协调解决防范和处置非法集资工作中的重大问题。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第七条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　各级人民政府应当合理保障防范和处置非法集资工作相关经费，并列入本级预算。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=center  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:0.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:center;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第二章　防　　范</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第八条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　地方各级人民政府应当建立非法集资监测预警机制，纳入社会治安综合治理体系，发挥网格化管理和基层群众自治组织的作用，运用大数据等现代信息技术手段，加强对非法集资的监测预警。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >行业主管部门、监管部门应当强化日常监督管理，负责本行业、领域非法集资的风险排查和监测预警。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >联席会议应当建立健全全国非法集资监测预警体系，推动建设国家监测预警平台，促进地方、部门信息共享，加强非法集资风险研判，及时预警提示。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第九条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　市场监督管理部门应当加强企业、个体工商户名称和经营范围等商事登记管理。除法律、行政法规和国家另有规定外，企业、个体工商户名称和经营范围中不得包含</font>&#8220;金融&#8221;、&#8220;交易所&#8221;、&#8220;交易中心&#8221;、&#8220;理财&#8221;、&#8220;财富管理&#8221;、&#8220;股权众筹&#8221;等字样或者内容。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >县级以上地方人民政府处置非法集资牵头部门、市场监督管理部门等有关部门应当建立会商机制，发现企业、个体工商户名称或者经营范围中包含前款规定以外的其他与集资有关的字样或者内容的，及时予以重点关注。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第十条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　处置非法集资牵头部门会同互联网信息内容管理部门、电信主管部门加强对涉嫌非法集资的互联网信息和网站、移动应用程序等互联网应用的监测。经处置非法集资牵头部门组织认定为用于非法集资的，互联网信息内容管理部门、电信主管部门应当及时依法作出处理。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >互联网信息服务提供者应当加强对用户发布信息的管理，不得制作、复制、发布、传播涉嫌非法集资的信息。发现涉嫌非法集资的信息，应当保存有关记录，并向处置非法集资牵头部门报告。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第十一条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　除国家另有规定外，任何单位和个人不得发布包含集资内容的广告或者以其他方式向社会公众进行集资宣传。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >市场监督管理部门会同处置非法集资牵头部门加强对涉嫌非法集资广告的监测。经处置非法集资牵头部门组织认定为非法集资的，市场监督管理部门应当及时依法查处相关非法集资广告。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >广告经营者、广告发布者应当依照法律、行政法规查验相关证明文件，核对广告内容。对没有相关证明文件且包含集资内容的广告，广告经营者不得提供设计、制作、代理服务，广告发布者不得发布。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第十二条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　处置非法集资牵头部门与所在地国务院金融管理部门分支机构、派出机构应当建立非法集资可疑资金监测机制。国务院金融管理部门及其分支机构、派出机构应当按照职责分工督促、指导金融机构、非银行支付机构加强对资金异常流动情况及其他涉嫌非法集资可疑资金的监测工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第十三条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　金融机构、非银行支付机构应当履行下列防范非法集资的义务：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >（一）建立健全内部管理制度，禁止分支机构和员工参与非法集资，防止他人利用其经营场所、销售渠道从事非法集资；</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >（二）加强对社会公众防范非法集资的宣传教育，在经营场所醒目位置设置警示标识；</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >（三）依法严格执行大额交易和可疑交易报告制度，对涉嫌非法集资资金异常流动的相关账户进行分析识别，并将有关情况及时报告所在地国务院金融管理部门分支机构、派出机构和处置非法集资牵头部门。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第十四条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　行业协会、商会应当加强行业自律管理、自我约束，督促、引导成员积极防范非法集资，不组织、不协助、不参与非法集资。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第十五条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　联席会议应当建立中央和地方上下联动的防范非法集资宣传教育工作机制，推动全国范围内防范非法集资宣传教育工作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >地方各级人民政府应当开展常态化的防范非法集资宣传教育工作，充分运用各类媒介或者载体，以法律政策解读、典型案例剖析、投资风险教育等方式，向社会公众宣传非法集资的违法性、危害性及其表现形式等，增强社会公众对非法集资的防范意识和识别能力。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >行业主管部门、监管部门以及行业协会、商会应当根据本行业、领域非法集资风险特点，有针对性地开展防范非法集资宣传教育活动。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >新闻媒体应当开展防范非法集资公益宣传，并依法对非法集资进行舆论监督。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第十六条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　对涉嫌非法集资行为，任何单位和个人有权向处置非法集资牵头部门或者其他有关部门举报。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >国家鼓励对涉嫌非法集资行为进行举报。处置非法集资牵头部门以及其他有关部门应当公开举报电话和邮箱等举报方式、在政府网站设置举报专栏，接受举报，及时依法处理，并为举报人保密。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第十七条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　居民委员会、村民委员会发现所在区域有涉嫌非法集资行为的，应当向当地人民政府、处置非法集资牵头部门或者其他有关部门报告。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第十八条</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >　处置非法集资牵头部门和行业主管部门、监管部门发现本行政区域或者本行业、领域可能存在非法集资风险的，有权对相关单位和个人进行警示约谈，责令整改。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=justify  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:21.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p> </o:p></span></p><p class=p  align=center  style="margin-top:0.0000pt;margin-right:0.0000pt;margin-bottom:0.0000pt;margin-left:0.0000pt;text-indent:0.0000pt;padding:0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt ;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;text-align:center;background:rgb(255,255,255);" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:仿宋;color:rgb(51,51,51);letter-spacing:0.0000pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;font-style:normal;font-size:15.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;background:rgb(255,255,255);mso-shading:rgb(255,255,255);" ><font face="仿宋" >第三章　处　　置</font></span></b><span
